Witcraft
  • Music
Palta in Hindustani Classical music is a set of rhythmic notes based on a permutational pattern in ascending and descending order. Driven by the need to create Palta for my practice and intrigued by the technical challenge it offered to my left‐brain, I wrote a comprehensive algorithm that can generate up to 3,000 Palta with a click of a button. Released here are about 750 Palta. Note that although all Swaras are pure and in basic Thāt Bilaval, these Palta can be practised within any Thāt.
Pattern: 12
1 – 2
Arohi – Avrohi (excludes higher octave notes)
S RR GG MM PP DD NN S’
S’ NN DD PP MM GG RR S
S RR GG MM PP DD NN S’
N S’D NP DM PG MR GS R‘N S
Arohi – Avrohi (includes higher octave notes)
S RR GG MM PP DD NN S’S’ R’R’ G’G’ M’
M’ G’G’ R’R’ S’S’ NN DD PP MM GG RR S
S RR GG MM PP DD NN S’S’ R’R’ G’G’ M’
G’ M’R’ G’S’ R’N S’D NP DM PG MR GS R‘N S
Pattern: 21

Arohi – Avrohi (includes higher octave notes)

G’ M’R’ G’S’ R’N S’D NP DM PG MR GS R‘N S
R SG RM GP MD PN DS’ NR’ S’G’ R’M’ G’
M’ G’G’ R’R’ S’S’ NN DD PP MM GG RR S
